 India and Pakistan announced on Friday that they had agreed to mutually resolve all issues regarding diplomats
 ek duusare ke rajanyikon ko sataae jane ke bare main donon deshon ke aarope- pratyarope ke baad yah sahmati bani he
 The Ministry of External Affairs said in a statement that on the lines of the Code of Conduct of Dealing with Diplomatic / Envoy Workers in India and Pakistan, the two countries have mutually agreed to resolve issues related to dealing with diplomats and diplomatic premises
 pakistan videsh karyaalay ne bhi isi tarah kaa ek bayaan jari kiya he

 india today anti phek news war room (AFWA) ne apni padtaal main paaya ki is viral video main kiya ja rahaa he daawa galat he
 Neither it is an Air India flight nor is Haj pilgrims sitting in it
 darasal ye video kam se kam teen saal purana he or 2016 se hi internet par gum rahaa he
 According to several previously published reports, it was a Saudi Arabian Airlines flight from Jeddah in Saudi Arabia to Addis Ababa, Ethiopia
 fasebuk pej “farzi Baaten” sahit kai yuzars ne is bhraamak post ko share kiya he
 Misleading claims made on social media are also trying to give this video a communal color as it is seen in the video that many people are wearing headgear that is usually worn by Muslims
